Chiang Tso-pin's Talk Upon Passing Through Shenyang 9

Many Matters to Report Upon This Return to the Country

German Industrial Delegation Has Excellent Impression of China

Soviet Russia's Five-Year Plan is About to Succeed

Shenyang Dispatch: Envoy to Germany, Chiang Tso-pin, departed from Germany to return to China, briefly staying in Soviet Russia to inspect its five-year industrial plan. On April 24th, he arrived in Harbin, and at 1:26 PM on the 26th, he arrived in Shenyang. The China Travel Agency had previously reserved Room 9 at the Lingge Hotel for him to stay in. Hu Weide and his wife also accompanied Chiang from Harbin. After Chiang disembarked, he went to the Eastern Mausoleum to tour the scenic spots. He returned to his residence around 5 PM. The next day (27th), he visited important Chinese and foreign figures in Shenyang. In the afternoon, at 4:30 PM, he visited Zang Shiyi, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, at the Provincial Government. A reporter interviewed Chiang at the Lingge Hotel. According to Chiang's remarks, he had many matters to report to the National Government upon his return, but as the time for disclosure had not yet arrived, he could not reveal them. He passed through Moscow and met with the Soviet Plenipotentiary three or four times. When he arrived in Moscow, it coincided with the third meeting of the Sino-Soviet Conference. Our side proposed a redemption plan for the Chinese Eastern Railway, and the Russian side also proposed a counter-proposal. The recent situation was very good. By the time the fourth meeting was held, I (Chiang referring to himself) had already set off to return to the country, so I have not yet heard the results. As for the progress of the conference, the Soviet Plenipotentiary sent telegrams to the Central Government from time to time. As for the railway redemption issue, we have lost many good opportunities in the past due to our Chinese people's self-deception, resulting in considerable losses. As for the German industrial delegation that came to China for inspection last year, they returned home with an excellent impression. However, they were surprised and expressed regret that China, an agricultural country with abundant agricultural products such as wheat and rice, still relies on foreign imports. They believed that if China's politics could get on the right track in the shortest possible time, it would definitely make significant progress. Germany, facing economic difficulties after the Great War, has no cash to invest in China. What they can use for investment are large quantities of machinery. The Soviet Union's efforts to govern with determination, setting aside empty talk and focusing on practical work, mean the five-year plan will soon succeed, which is worthy of the world's attention. The deep historical and geographical relationship between China and Russia is especially worthy of our study. In the world panic, with capitalism and socialism mutually squeezing each other, capitalism is not easily destroyed, and socialism's ability to emerge is also due to its own strength. If the Soviet Union's five-year plan succeeds, the world will definitely feel the impact. In studying any doctrine, we must always study it with the eyes of a scholar. For example, reading Marx's theory does not necessarily mean following Marx's theory. Research and practice are two different things. Chiang also stated that this return to the country is a customary practice for diplomats, as he had been abroad for several years and urgently needed to return for a trip. Moreover, there are many diplomatic secrets that cannot be conveyed by written messages and must be reported in person. Currently, the international attitude towards China still does not deviate from its coordinated strategy and is unwilling to take unilateral action. Therefore, if our country wants to save itself, it must not hope for assistance from any one country, but must rely on the joint efforts of all the people of the country to succeed. (April 27th)

Ministry of Interior 10

Promulgates Outline for County and District Consolidation

Orders Provinces to Investigate and Report on Schedule

The 18th State Council meeting of the Executive Yuan, based on the resolutions of the National Interior Affairs Conference, decided on a ten-article outline for the consolidation of county administrative regions. Yesterday, it ordered the Ministry of Interior to forward it to the provincial governments' civil affairs departments for strict compliance and reporting. The Ministry of Interior immediately issued a notice to the provinces, stating: "The National Interior Affairs Conference resolved that the Hebei Provincial Government's proposal to survey and demarcate the inter-provincial and inter-county 'flower-patch' lands to clarify boundaries and unify political power; the Henan Provincial Department of Civil Affairs' proposal to survey and determine flower-planting sections and transfer them to the jurisdiction of the counties where they are located to unify authority and benefit administration; and the Ministry of Interior's Civil Affairs Department's proposal to consolidate the administrative regions of counties throughout the country were all discussed and resolved in a consolidated manner, with the principle being passed and sent to the Ministry of Interior to formulate detailed basic measures for distribution to the provinces for strict compliance, etc., as recorded in the minutes. After the closing of the conference, the Guizhou Provincial Department of Civil Affairs submitted a proposal to issue a general order to the provinces to re-survey and correct provincial boundaries in accordance with the Boundary Survey Regulations for the purpose of governance, the content of which is largely the same as the previous three proposals, and should be handled together. After detailed review, the administrative regions of counties in our country have followed the old system of the Ming and Qing dynasties, and the boundaries are extremely intricate, which is extremely inconvenient for governance. As the original text of each proposal states, the Ministry has seen this before and has drafted the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations as the standard for establishing boundaries, which has been approved and promulgated for implementation. Now is the time when the country is vigorously implementing autonomy, and the county is the unit of autonomy. If the boundaries are not uniform, there will be many obstacles when delineating autonomous regions. Moreover, since the case of reorganizing provincial districts has been decided by the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee for preparation, it is necessary to start by consolidating county districts to avoid the evils of Hua being separated. The National Interior Affairs Conference's proposals on surveying 'flower-patch' lands have been unanimously approved by representatives of the provincial governments, and there should be no obstacles or difficulties in implementation. The Ministry has, based on the resolutions, drafted an outline of measures for consolidating county administrative regions as a supplementary measure to the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations, which has been submitted to the Executive Yuan. On April 2nd of this year, Directive No. 1103 was submitted to the 18th State Council meeting, which resolved to approve it. In addition to distributing it separately, we enclose twenty copies of the outline of measures for consolidating county administrative regions and three copies of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations and request your esteemed provincial government to investigate, instruct compliance, and report back. This is to all provincial governments."

Attached is the Outline of Measures for Consolidating County Administrative Regions as follows: 1. In addition to complying with the provisions of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations, the consolidation of county administrative regions shall be carried out in accordance with this outline of measures. 2. If the administrative region of a county has any of the circumstances listed in Article 7 of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations and administrative inconvenience is felt, it should be immediately and earnestly consolidated. 3. Consolidation measures are as follows: (1) Straighten out the boundaries where the borders of adjacent counties intersect, so that they are neat and not uneven. (2) Exchange parts of adjacent counties for the convenience of jurisdiction and terrain. (3) Divide counties with vast land and difficult administration into two counties or merge part of them into other counties for the convenience of governance. (4) Merge parts of several counties to establish new county seats, or abolish old county seats and merge them with other counties to form new counties. The principles of consolidation shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations. 4. Within three months of the promulgation of these measures, the civil affairs departments of each province shall thoroughly investigate and list in detail whether the administrative regions of the counties under their jurisdiction have any of the circumstances listed in Article 7 of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations, and formulate a consolidation plan with drawings and explanations, which shall be reported by the provincial government to the Ministry of Interior for verification. 5. After the civil affairs departments of each province have investigated, drafted, and reported to the Ministry, they shall immediately and earnestly implement the proposed consolidation plan within the shortest possible time. If it involves two or more provinces, the civil affairs departments concerned shall, with the approval of their respective provincial governments, consult and handle it. 6. If the consolidation of county administrative regions can be decided by agreement without the need for on-site surveying, the civil affairs department concerned shall report the case to the authorities for approval in accordance with the procedures. If it involves two or more provinces, the provincial governments concerned shall jointly consult the Ministry and submit a report for approval. 7. If on-site surveying is required for the consolidation of county administrative regions, the surveying procedures stipulated in Articles 8 and 9 of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations shall still be followed. 8. After the redrawing of the county administrative regions is finalized, boundary markers shall be erected on the newly drawn boundary lines in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the Provincial, Municipal, and County Boundary Survey Regulations. 9. After the redrawing of the county administrative regions, the original population, taxes, documents, registers, official property, public property, schools, bureaus, charitable organizations, temples, scenic spots, historical sites, cultural relics, etc., shall be transferred to the jurisdiction of the new area. However, the occupational rights of the people shall remain as before. 10. These measures shall also apply to the establishment of administrative bureaus.

Liu Zhi Passes Through Xuzhou to Go to the Capital 11

Attends National Assembly and Reports on Henan's Situation

Liu Qiyao Initiates Construction of Xuguan Railway

Xuzhou Dispatch: Liu Zhi, in order to attend the National Assembly, departed from Bian in Henan on the morning of April 30th, accompanied by Li Zhenfeng, Secretary of the Henan Provincial Government, Wu Dunsheng, Secretary of the Military Headquarters, and others. He arrived in Xuzhou at 4 PM. Wang Jun, along with representatives from all sectors of the local community, welcomed him at the station and boarded the train to speak with Liu. Liu stated that in addition to attending the National Assembly, he would also report on the military and political situation in Henan. The important political affairs in Henan are currently focused on two paths: village clearing and local self-government. The bandit Cui Erdan's gang is causing trouble in western Henan and is being suppressed by Zhang Fang and Li Yunjie's troops. A group of communist bandits in southern Henan is also being suppressed by Ji Hongchang's troops. Self-government in various counties is being implemented in order. During the conversation, he inquired about the reported issue of dividing Xuhai into a province. The representatives requested that Liu make a strong argument in the National Assembly for dividing Xuhai into a province. Liu expressed his permission to study it. Liu Qiyao, a member of the Henan Provincial Party, was traveling with Liu. Liu has recently been the initiator of the Xuguan Railway. He went to Beijing to proceed with the filing with the Ministry of Railways. The reporter inquired with Liu about the origins of the Xuguan Railway. Liu replied that transportation in western Henan is blocked, making it difficult to implement village clearing and administration. The people there are particularly suffering. Now, the people are spontaneously initiating the construction of a railway to develop transportation in western Henan. The route is set to pass through Xuchang, Xiangcheng, Yexian, Fangcheng, Nanyang, Dengxian, and finally Guanghua (i.e., Laohekou), with a length of 640 li and an estimated cost of 22 million yuan. It is planned to raise all private shares, with two-thirds coming from land, divided into direct, indirect, and ordinary shares, and one-third raised from merchants and domestic investors, all of which will be used as capital. Currently, the people of each county concerned recognize the necessity of building the road and are happy to invest. Recently, if the railway construction plan is approved by the Ministry of Railways, construction can begin. I, representing the initiators, have prepared a plan to submit to the ministry, etc. Liu Zhi's special train then headed south at 6 PM. (30th)

Zhang Zhijiang Announces剿匪Situation 13

Yangzhou Dispatch: The Jiangsu Pacification and Rehabilitation Association recently sent a letter to the Jiangsu Pacification Supervisor's Office requesting details of the recent bandit suppression situation in order to jointly devise a plan for action. It is reported that the Supervisor's Office has replied to the Association, stating that the Supervisor's Office's pacification policy is divided into two types. For organized bandits, the main method is to use troops to encircle and suppress them. For scattered and sporadic bandits hiding in various counties, the county police teams are ordered to conduct strict searches and suppress them. At the same time, the county magistrates are ordered to begin village clearing. After the initial four months of pacification work, the large bandit gangs in the Xuhuaihai area were gradually eliminated. Currently, there are still remnants of Wei Yousan's gang, numbering five or six hundred, who are gathering in the area bordering Su, Wan, and the intersection of Sui, Su, Wan, and Si counties. When the second phase of pacification work began, Zhang Zhan魁, commander of the 3rd Cavalry Division, joined forces with Liu's Brigade of the 25th Route Army and the garrison in Wan and Si counties, as well as the Xuzhou troops, to jointly encircle and suppress them. On the 2nd of this month, Commander Zhang telegraphed that the bandits had occupied more than twenty Zhuang villages in the areas of Bao Wei, Zhao Gou, and Da Xiao Yangjia Wei in the three counties of Suichuan and Wan and Si. There were two fierce battles with the bandits, killing more than fifty bandits, capturing more than twenty bandits, and seizing more than ten guns. Two officers, one horse, and six soldiers of the division were killed, and one regimental commander and more than ten soldiers were wounded. More than ten hostages were rescued. The encirclement and suppression are still continuing, and a plan for thoroughly eliminating the bandits has been drafted and submitted by the Supervisor's Office to Chief Commander Liang for overall planning and implementation. The Governor of Anhui has also been telegraphed to send troops to encircle and suppress the bandits in the Wan and Si area. It is expected that the bandits can be eliminated in half a month. Secondly, the sea bandits in the Tonghaiyan area are currently being jointly suppressed by the 25th Route Army, the Provincial Police, and the Navy. Thirdly, the bandits in the Maoshan area of Jurong are currently being searched and suppressed by Li Changjiang, commander of the Ningzhen District. Fourthly, the bandits in Taihu Lake have already had a village clearing and bandit suppression plan drafted by the Supervisor's Office. It is necessary to wait until the Provincial Maritime Public Security has eliminated the sea bandits in the Tonghaiyan area and the coastal areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang before concentrating the full force of the water police to carry out a comprehensive suppression. As for the sporadic bandits in other counties, efforts are being made to supervise and urge the counties to carry out village clearing and suppression, with the aim of completing the village clearing work throughout the province during this pacification period.

Han Fuju 14

Orders Village Clearing in Counties of Southern Shandong

Remnants of Bandits from Baodugu Flee to Lincheng

Jinan Dispatch: Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuju, believing that the bandits in Baodugu are gradually being suppressed, and that the counties in the bandit areas of southern Shandong should urgently carry out village clearing and rehabilitation to eradicate the roots of banditry, telegraphed Liu Shuxiang, Chief of Staff of the Third Route Army stationed in Tengxian, on April 29th, ordering the magistrates of Yixian, Linqu, Feixian, Tengxian, and Yixian to supervise and lead the local militias to promptly carry out village clearing and post-rehabilitation work. Liu has already complied with the order and sent a telegraph reply. The Chief of Staff's Office in Tengxian also sent a telegraph reporting the discovery of a band of bandits near Lincheng and reporting on the situation of searching and suppressing hidden bandits in Baodugu. Excerpts from the telegraphs are as follows: (1) Telegraph: Received with respect. I have already ordered the magistrates of Linqu, Feixian, Tengxian, and Yixian to supervise and lead the local militias to promptly carry out village clearing and post-rehabilitation work and report back at any time. (2) (According to Army Commander Wang) All (Telegraph notified that a band of bandits had been discovered near Lincheng. After investigation, they were found to be fleeing after being severely attacked by Gu's division and Ma's brigade during the Yin and Yang days. Many have been captured by the Lian Zhuang Hui (Joint Village Association) here. In addition to ordering strict searches in various counties, I have also issued orders to the various units at the front to pay attention to defense. (3) According to Division Commander Chen's urgent telegram (A) According to Regimental Commander Guo's report, a band of four or five hundred bandits was discovered at the Hanziyu Pass. They engaged in a fierce battle with the Second Battalion of the regiment for two hours. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and fled to Jiaoshankeng in the northeast. Twelve were killed on the spot, thirty guns and seven hostages were captured. Two soldiers of our side were killed and one wounded. According to a follow-up report from the regimental commander, there are bandits of varying numbers in Xiangshandong, Jiaoshuidong, and Longzhuadong. The regiment has dispatched troops to encircle and suppress them separately, but there are too few soldiers and too many caves to allocate enough. (B) According to Regimental Commander Xu, there are many mountain caves in the Zhangyuzi, Sunjiayuzi, Liyuzi, Zhuwo, and Manshantou areas, but no bandits have been found. (C) The division's Regimental Commander Xu is stationed in Xizhuang, and Xu Ying is stationed in Gaozhuang to provide reinforcements as needed.

Han Fuju stated to reporters today that, according to repeated reports from the various units at the front, the bandits in Baodugu have been routed and are currently engaged in searching and suppressing sporadic small groups. They should be able to be eliminated within three to five days. However, there are many mountains and caves near Baodugu, and there are caves everywhere. There are also entrances and exits with interconnected caves. The large caves can accommodate thirty to fifty people, or even hundreds. The bandits are familiar with the geography, and the caves are covered with stone. The search and suppression work is not easy. I have telegraphed the various units to actively search and leave troops as appropriate to allocate forces for bandit suppression in order to permanently eliminate the suffering in southern Shandong. Also, the 29th Division of Cao Fulin's troops and the 20th Division of Sun Tongxuan's troops have rotated their defenses. Cao led the division's various departments and subordinate units on two trains from Qingzhou back to Ji on the 29th. Ma Jingong, commander of the 60th Brigade of Sun's 20th Division, led his troops on three trains through Ji to Qingzhou on the 29th.

Liaoning Province Implements Business Tax 15

Shenyang Chamber of Commerce Submits a Consultation Letter

Shenyang Dispatch: Liaoning Province has scheduled to implement business tax on May 1st, as previously reported. The new tax regulations, implementation rules, and penalties were formulated in advance by the Department of Finance in accordance with the guidelines issued by the National Government and the resolutions of the Northeast Finance Conference, taking into account the special circumstances of Liaoning Province, and submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for deliberation and approval. Subsequently, at a provincial tax conference convened by the Department of Finance, the directors of tax bureaus from various counties attended and discussed the new tax rules in detail. Minor amendments were made to the various articles. After review and clarification by the Department of Finance, it was submitted to the Provincial Government for approval by the Ministry of Finance. It was decided to collect the new tax on May 1st and sent a letter to the chambers of commerce of various counties and cities throughout the province to inform merchants to comply with the new tax rules and pay the tax. The Shenyang Chamber of Commerce, considering the impact of the new tax on the interests of merchants, organized a committee to conduct a thorough study and drafted a consultation letter. After receiving the aforementioned notice, it convened a meeting of various trade associations at 10 a.m. on the 29th to jointly discuss it. The meeting closed at 4 p.m. and approved the consultation letter. On the one hand, it complied with the new regulations to pay taxes. On the other hand, it requested the Department of Finance to adopt and implement them. The Liaoning Provincial Department of Finance's order to collect business tax is recorded below. It is ordered that the lijin tax be abolished and replaced with business tax, which has long been ordered by the National Government to be implemented nationwide within a time limit. However, at this time when the tax system is being reformed, there are many aspects to consider. If we do not carefully examine them, I am afraid that we will cause more obstacles. The Department of Finance, seeing this, has followed the guidelines issued by the National Government and the resolutions of the Northeast Finance Conference, taking into account the special circumstances of this province, and has carefully and thoroughly formulated various implementation rules for the business tax and submitted them to the Provincial Committee for deliberation and approval. The preparations are now complete, and implementation will begin on May 1st. The original sales tax in this province will be abolished from the same day to avoid double taxation. However, merchants must still pay business tax on goods that were previously stored and have already paid sales tax after they are sold. They must not deduct it to prevent abuse. From now on, all merchants must deeply understand the overall situation and strictly abide by the regulations. They must also know that paying taxes is a national obligation. If they violate the regulations or engage in fraudulent practices, they will be punished according to the law. As for tax officials who cause difficulties or extort money, they will be reported at any time, and the head of the Department will severely punish them according to the law and will not tolerate them. In addition to reporting to the authorities, the Department orders the bureau to comply with the order and issue a public notice to inform the merchants.

The rent for the foreign concessions in Wuhu has always been calculated in cash. The Wuhu Public Security Bureau has recently, due to the fact that the annual grain and various surcharges have increased more than double and the price of money has fallen sharply, resulting in a virtual decrease in revenue that is insufficient to cover expenses, has notified the consuls of various countries in accordance with Article 7 of the Public Concession Regulations of various countries that, starting from this year, the rent for each mu of land will be uniformly changed to three silver dollars.

Reporters from various newspapers stationed in Wuhu, including those from Beijing, Shanghai, and Wuhan, have organized a Wuhu Reporters' Group on Zhongshan Road on the 1st in order to connect emotions and enhance reporting strength.

The Anhui Coastal Anti-Smuggling Commissioner's Office was ordered to close at the end of April. All Anhui coastal anti-smuggling and the Independent Second Battalion of the Special Tax Police Regiment of the Ministry of Finance stationed in Wuhu will be managed by the Anhui Coastal Audit Office from May 1st.

The Anhui business tax will be levied starting from May 1st. Wuhu Commissioner Feng Enpu convened a joint deliberation meeting with the County Chamber of Commerce, the County Government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Finance Bureau. It was resolved to send a letter to the County Higher Association to convene merchants in the association to urge them to submit applications. Merchants who have not joined the association will be urged to pay by the Commissioner with the cooperation of the police.

Local Dispatch

Songjiang 18

Sentencing of Kidnappers in the Sun Case of Xin Zhuang:

Sun Xiangyun, a wealthy farmer from Xin Zhuang, was kidnapped and held for ransom on the evening of May 21st the year before last. He was transferred and hidden without a trace. Subsequently, the First Team of the First District of the Water Police of the Provincial Public Security Bureau captured Huang Miaogen, Liu Asi, Shen Ayou, Yu Bugen, Yang Jinsheng, Lu Jinlin, Jiang Zhicheng, and others. Sun Xiangyun's wife, Sun Xu, and daughter, Sun Baozhen, accused Sun Shoumei, a relative who had once been a primary school teacher, of being involved in the kidnapping. During the apprehension, Jiang Zhicheng confessed to hiding the kidnap victim in a house in Pudong. The Water Police were dispatched to rescue him. However, while passing through Minhang, Jiang Zhicheng jumped into the river and drowned. From then on, Sun Xiangyun disappeared without a trace. The above-mentioned criminals were interrogated by the County Government, which also handled judicial matters. After the County Court was established, except for Shen Ayou, who was executed by the County, the entire case was transferred. After repeated investigations, a public prosecution was initiated. The Criminal Court conducted a public trial and delivered a verdict. Huang Miaogen and Liu Asi were each sentenced to death for the crime of jointly kidnapping and holding for ransom and were deprived of their civil rights for life. Yu Bugen was given a reduced sentence of life imprisonment and was deprived of his civil rights for life. Yang Jinsheng and Lu Jinlin were each sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment and were deprived of their civil rights for fifteen years. The number of days of pre-trial detention were counted as two days equaling one day of imprisonment. Sun Shoumei was declared innocent.

Songjin Daily to be Published Regularly:

Local enthusiasts from Songjiang and Jinshan counties, lamenting the lack of public opinion in the two counties, initiated the organization of the Songjin Daily and raised a fund of three thousand yuan. Half of the funds have already been raised. Yesterday, an inaugural meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce, and Ban Shisheng, Cai Zhongyu, Bao Zheng, and Deputy President Gao Junfan were elected as directors. The Commercial Printing Company in the city was commissioned to print the newspaper, which is scheduled to be published on the tenth of this month.

Wuxi

Fifth Precinct Uncovers a Major Gambling Den:

The Sheqiao area on Tonghui Road in this city has unexpectedly become a silk factory. Now that the factory is closed, most of the staff have nothing to do, so they spend their days gambling heavily, shouting and betting on games such as "sand crab," "pai gow," and mahjong, with significant wins and losses. After a secret report, the Fifth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau sent police to investigate and arrest twenty-one gamblers on the spot, including Yang Runquan and others. They were immediately taken to the precinct, where Precinct Chief Peng held a preliminary hearing and ordered them to be detained. Just as he was preparing to transfer the case to the General Bureau, a person named Qian Pin'san arrived at the precinct and requested that the transfer be waived. Qian then arranged for the gamblers to raise four hundred yuan as a settlement condition, and all the gamblers were released.

Further Arrests in the Xidu Jialian Robbery Case:

Zhou Jiashan, the chief of the Eighth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau in this city, has spared no effort in apprehending bandits. The other day, he personally led police officers, including Du Bingnan, disguised as fishermen, and hired a fishing boat to sail to Yuanfu Bay near Zhoutan Bridge in Xin'an Township to investigate. They successfully arrested Zhu Genda, a major suspect in the Xidu Jialian robbery case. He was immediately taken to the precinct for interrogation. The suspect confessed that he was thirty years old, a farmer. He first participated in robberies in September of last year at the homes of Zhou Badou and Zhou Jingsheng in Shitangwan. Last month, he went to Miaoxia to rob the homes of Xu Xiaofu, Zhang Yutou, and Amei. He received three yuan. In the Xidu Jialian robbery case, there were twelve people involved, and he received thirty yuan, and so on. After reviewing the confession, Chief Zhou prepared a document yesterday and submitted it to the County Government for legal action.

Establishment of the County Relief Institute:

The establishment of the Wuxi County Relief Institute was previously decided upon by the County Administrative Council. Subsequently, the County Political Council appointed a director to be responsible for preparing the institute and drafted regulations, which were submitted to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval and filing. The institute is organized by combining the existing Tongrentang, Yuyingtang, Pujitang, and Pingmin Xiyisuo, among others. It was formally established and began operations on May 1st. The office is rented at Tongrentang. Yesterday, the director, Yang Hanxi, and the deputy director, Qin Lianggong, submitted the establishment date and process to the county for filing.

Important Meeting of Silk Factories:

Yesterday, the Silk Factories Guild held a special members' meeting to discuss the allocation of silk industry bonds. Representatives from thirty-seven factories attended. It was resolved: 1. The two hundred thousand yuan of silk industry bonds for improving machinery should be allocated according to the number of vehicles currently owned by each factory in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai. Each factory should reclaim the funds themselves for improving machinery. Using the funds for other purposes will be opposed. 2. Given the extreme slump in the silk market, rental factories should request that landlords reduce rents, and the Shanghai model should be followed until the new cocoons are used. The meeting also discussed issues such as business tax. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Changzhou

Various Industries Oppose the Imposition of Business Tax:

On the 2nd, the silk, cloth, fur, and thread guilds, along with twenty-eight other industries in Wu County, sent a telegram to the Legislative Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Provincial Government and Department of Finance, stating that the Jiangsu Province Business Tax Regulations exceeded the provisions of the Ministry's outline in many ways. Although the regulations have been revised by the Ministry of Finance, they are still excessively harsh and disruptive to the people. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, without regard to the circumstances, immediately scheduled the implementation, causing public outrage. The associations have jointly resolved that they will not recognize the implementation order until the Central Business Tax Law is promulgated. They have filed a joint petition requesting a review and immediate order to stop the tax in order to appease public sentiment and maintain the legal system. They are anxiously awaiting orders.

Shenxin No. 6 Factory Warehouse Suffers Carelessness:

At 12:45 p.m. on the afternoon of the 2nd, a fire suddenly broke out in the northern stack room where the Shenxin No. 6 Factory outside Xiaonanmen in Wu County was storing printed cloth. Fire trucks from various districts rushed to the scene to put out the fire. However, because the room was filled with large amounts of printed cloth, about eight rooms were burned down, and all the printed cloth inside was destroyed. The fire spread to the neighboring house of Zhuang Longda, burning down three flat houses. It took about two hours for the fire to be put out. The Shenxin factory's losses are estimated at around 40,000 yuan. The cause of the fire is still unknown. However, the factory has fire insurance, so there should be considerable compensation.

Changshu

New Trial Judge Has Arrived in Changshu:

Gu Yushang, the trial judge of this county, has requested the High Court to resign from his position due to the difficulty of handling cases. Chai Zupeng, a candidate judge from the Wujin District Court, has been appointed to fill the vacancy.

Water Police Capture a Large Group of Bandits:

The patrol boat of the Thirteenth Water Police Team of this county was patrolling the middle reaches of Zhoutang on the Suchang line when, on the afternoon of the 1st, while passing through the Lumu Tang area in the Su border, they received a secret report that there was a suspicious vessel near Tingzihang. The platoon leader of the first detachment patrol ship, Hu Jinbiao, went to investigate and found the boat owner, Liu Xiao'er, his partner, Zhu A'er, and several women. Because they were indeed suspicious, they were taken back to the patrol boat for questioning. Liu Xiao'er confessed that he was not a bandit but admitted to petty theft in the village and had some knowledge of the main culprits who robbed the Yongyichang and Yongyixiang letter ships. Commander Hu took Liu and the others to Changshu and reported the situation to Ni Zuoyou, the platoon leader of the first detachment. Upon hearing this, Ni dispatched more patrol boats and led Liu Xiao'er and others to Dongtang City, where they arrested Yang Xiaolao in a small wine shop. Then, they went to Hengjing Xibaishui's noodle shop to check three boats. Only women and children were found on board. They said that the men had all gone ashore. The patrol boats secretly guarded the vicinity, and soon they arrested Yang Xiaobao, Wang Xiaolao Han, and Li Xiaolao (i.e., Wenlin), among others, who claimed to make a living by hunting birds and dared not be bandits. Two bird guns, a gray serge jacket, a green cashmere headband shirt, a toadskin crepe trousers, a serge trousers, a moon-white du cloth, and a white oblique-striped short shirt were found on the boat. The detachment believed that these stolen goods were related to the case and, together with the suspects, were escorted to the city and reported to the team headquarters. Unexpectedly, at around eight o'clock, while passing through Yangcheng Lake, they suddenly saw two net boats approaching. They ordered an inspection, but two shots were suddenly fired from the net boats. The police knew there was a change and also fired shots to warn them. The bandits, knowing that the police were prepared, tried to escape into the port on the left side but were chased and captured by the police. Wu Baocai, Sun Yigui, Li Wentian, Zhu Tongyu, and the boatman, Li Laolao, were arrested that night and taken back to the team headquarters. After detailed questioning by detachment leader Ni, they all confessed to robbing the letter ship of the People's Letter Bureau in Zhangjiadian on February 19th. Detachment leader Ni briefly interrogated them and temporarily detained them at the team headquarters, scheduling them to be transferred to the Thirteenth Team headquarters for transfer to the County Judiciary for interrogation in three days.

Nantong

Military Police Search and Arrest Ambush Bandits Along the Coast:

The coastal bandits in Lvsi Sanyu and other areas along the coast of Jiangbei have been suppressed by the fishing protection and bandit suppression military police. However, there are still ambush bandits who have not been cleared. On the 2nd, the 282nd Regiment and the Security Police Team joined forces with the water patrols to conduct a thorough search and arrested three key bandits, Cao Shou and others. The evidence was conclusive, and they were immediately executed at the Beiyang Bridge entrance.

Automobile Tax Issues in Various Counties in Jiangbei:

The Construction Department has newly stipulated that the business automobile tax is ten yuan per vehicle per month, and a security deposit of one hundred yuan must be paid. The automobile industry in various counties in Jiangbei unanimously opposed this. The Construction Department convened a meeting of the Construction Bureau chiefs of various counties to discuss the following: (1) The monthly tax for ordinary business automobiles in this county and neighboring counties shall be handled in accordance with the new regulations. (2) For the security deposit of ordinary business automobiles, those that were established before January of the 20th year shall have their security deposit changed to a general store guarantee of five hundred yuan. Those established after January of the 20th year shall be handled in accordance with the new regulations. (3) The issuance of ordinary business automobile licenses in each county shall be suspended. However, the automobile industry shall continue to request a reduction in taxes. Bandits Captured in Pingchao Escorted to the County:

On the 2nd, the county police team escorted seven bandits captured in Pingchao, Ke Xiaodong, Gu Bingcheng, Qian Jin, Ma Tuzi, Lu Sheng, Chen Bing, and Zhou Hai, to the County Government for interrogation.

Zhenjiang

Representatives of the Jiangsu People's Assembly Request Gu Regarding Business Tax Issues:

Representatives of industrial groups and the People's Assembly of Jiangsu Province gathered in the provincial capital on the 1st to obtain credentials. Afterwards, they held a discussion on the business tax issue at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce. They generally agreed that since the Jiangsu Province government had decided to impose the business tax, it would be difficult to delay it further. However, the business tax law is currently being drafted in the Legislative Yuan, and the level of the tax rate is extremely important. They decided to summarize the previous requests into the following six points: (1) The tax rate should be calculated equally using the per-mille method, regardless of whether the business capital exceeds two per mille. (2) The collection period should follow the decision of the national conference on streamlining levies in 1928. The first article of the business tax outline stipulated that the business license should be renewed annually, and the tax amount should be calculated on an annual basis. Therefore, it should be divided into two installments per year, the first and second halves, following the busy season method. (3) Late payment fines should follow the busy season method, with an additional 10% late payment fine for payments overdue by more than two months. For those who evade taxes, in addition to being ordered to pay supplementary taxes, they should be dealt with in accordance with the regulations on penalties for violations of police regulations. The provisions of the Jiangsu Province regulations on suspending business operations and the Jiangsu Province Provisional Rules on Penalties for Business Tax, which stipulate excessively severe penalties, should be revoked. (4) According to the first article of the national conference on streamlining levies' decision on the business tax outline, companies that have already paid income tax to the central government and those that have already been levied special taxes by the central government are not within the scope of business tax collection by the provinces. Therefore, those who sell goods that have already been subject to unified tax and special tax and their direct products should not be subject to business tax again. (5) Wholesale businesses are wholesale in nature and should be exempt from tax. If there is a combination of wholesale and retail, only the retail business should be taxed. (6) The business license is a tax payment certificate issued by the government to merchants after they pay taxes, similar to the busy season plate, and should not be subject to stamp tax again. After the principles of the above requests were decided, Yu Xiao Chuan, Qian Sun Qing, Li Sheng Bo, Wang Jing Ting, Lan Bo Hua, and Zhang Shou Yi jointly sent a telegram to the Legislative Yuan on the 2nd, requesting that the above opinions be incorporated when drafting the business tax law. They also scheduled to go to the Legislative Yuan on the 4th to make their request.

Free Talk

Words of Insight 19

— Qiushui

A lover, like houses and objects, comes in two different kinds: one is extremely practical and can be enjoyed for a lifetime, and the other is a beautiful but useless luxury.

The only thing that can make a modern girl blush is when someone publicly says that she has never kissed a man.

A perfect lover and a good husband are not born like poets, but must be made by human effort. And who is their opponent? The women or wives who will become their wives.

The only virtue men possess is their ability to restrain their impulses and resist external temptations.

"Beautiful face" is the only praise given to a woman, and "perfect life" is the only conclusion to a man.

Only revolution can make a man a true and great man, and a true revolutionary will never stick to the old ways.

If a person wants to murder a tiger, he calls it sport. If a tiger wants to murder a person, we say it is bestiality. So-called justice and so-called sin have no definite standards.

A person can never become a pure expert unless he devotes himself to a certain field of study and becomes an idiot.

Every dream is a prediction, and every guess, after the erosion of time, can become a reality.

Liu Yazi's Autumn Lament in Moling 20

— Zizai

Ms. Zhang Qiushi from Wujiang has lofty aspirations and devotes herself to the revolution. Her perseverance has always been admired by her peers. In the past, she worked very hard in Shanghai and Nanjing, and was tragically killed by the enemy in Bai Xia. Her friend Liu Yazi was particularly grief-stricken. Yazi is a warm-hearted person. In the past, he presided over the Nanshe, and his literary talent was elegant and flowing, implicitly holding the reins of the literary circles in the southeast. If a member of the society suffered misfortune and their family was too poor to print their posthumous collection, he would often pay for it out of his own pocket. Many commentators praised his chivalrous deeds. How could he be indifferent to Ms. Zhang's tragic death? He built a tomb with clothes and hats next to Wuduo Temple in his hometown of Fenhu, and commissioned Chen Shuren and other faithful artists to paint two "Autumn Lament in Moling" paintings, widely soliciting poems and inscriptions. Many Chinese compatriots donated their own poems and inscriptions. Yazi successively composed more than a hundred poems, sighing repeatedly with tears of blood. I especially love to read his lyrics in the tune of "Touching the Fish" in the style of Ms. Lu Bicheng's "Elegy for London." Yazi's grief and indignation fill his chest, and his determination to avenge his friend is like ten thousand rays of golden light, with the aura of a sword piercing the sky, fully revealed between the lines. If Qiushi had any knowledge after her death, she would be grateful to her confidant, which would bring her some comfort and allow her to close her eyes in peace. The lyrics say: "Sigh, the west wind blows again in Bai Xia, the tomb of Pingling is filled with yellow calves, sadly playing the national anthem, how much blood of Chang Hong. Not the beans cooked from the same stalk, the turmoil suddenly pains a generation of beautiful women. To die at the hands of a brute is a disgrace. Heaven does not grant longevity to the upright. The round figure of the moon is replaced by the heroic figure of the cloud. At the age of thirty-nine, she knocks on the door to ask. At the time of the wailing at the new pavilion, Bo Ren pitied me for lightly betraying Ma Wei, the white silk strangled her throat, a tragic end, more shameful than a man's beheading. I resent my sleeves. Alas, the dragon sword is buried and cannot be drawn to take the enemy's head. Will the hero repent? But the bells and fish of Tongtai, the cool Brahmin chants, piously worship the King of Emptiness."

New Citizens of the Sea Rescue Friends in Distress 21

— Xin Wei

The Huayang ship of the Hang'an Company had an accident in the waters of Wenzhou. Details have been published in major newspapers. Yesterday, Zhang Jisheng, the second buyer on board the ship, returned to Shanghai and said that the lives of all the people on board were saved by pirates. Otherwise, everyone would have died. The incident was so strange that I recorded it as follows:

Pirates Reclaim the Desert Island:

Nan Yushan is isolated in the sea and inaccessible. The mountain is all stone, with no grass or trees growing, so it can be called a barren land. Every day, it is only friends with the waves and giant waves. The area of the mountain is quite large, but no one lives there. Liang Meiting, a pirate from Huangyan, Zhejiang, has been rampaging the ocean for more than ten years. He has many followers. In recent years, Liang has had a great change of heart and abandoned his life of robbery, transforming himself into a good citizen engaged in farming and fishing. Fearing that his followers would harm others if they were scattered, Liang gathered his subordinates and occupied this inaccessible desert island. He chose a place on the island to cultivate land, plant vegetables, and cultivate fruit, and went to sea to fish for a living. Over the years, the thatched huts with bamboo fences on this desert island have been filled with the crowing of chickens and the barking of dogs, becoming a new world on the sea.

Rescuing the Distressed:

The island is surrounded by high peaks, all with thousand-foot cliffs and no mountain paths that can be traversed. Liang Meiting abandoned his life of piracy and lived peacefully on the island, gathering a group of desperados to become new citizens of the sea. He is truly one who "lays down the butcher knife and becomes a Buddha on the spot." This time, the Huayang ship ran aground below the island. After the crew and passengers were rescued to the foot of the mountain, Liang Meiting led the residents of the island to rescue them. They all had three or four pistols on their bodies. The crew and passengers knew that they had met pirates and resigned themselves to death. To their surprise, Liang Meiting immediately declared to the crowd that he used to be a pirate but now he farms and is a good citizen. He came to rescue them sincerely and would not harm them. If they did not believe him, he was willing to swear to heaven and abandon his pistols. Then, he helped them up the mountain. The mountain was high and there was no road. Men could still use their hands and feet to climb like snakes, but many female passengers and children could not climb the mountain. Therefore, Liang Meiting ordered his wives and children to go down the mountain and carry them up on their backs.

Providing Food and Shelter to Friends in Distress:

The crew members still say that it was very dangerous to enter the mountain. Many of their fingernails fell off and their hands and feet were broken. After entering the mountain, they saw that the island was very large and had many thatched huts. Liang Meiting led one hundred and fourteen distressed friends to live in the thatched huts, providing them with food and bedding on the ground. That day, there was a strong wind and heavy rain. If Liang and his people had not rescued them, these hundred or so people would have had no hope of survival. The next day, the British ship came to rescue them. Liang personally escorted the distressed friends down the mountain. Those who were injured and could not walk were carried to the foot of the mountain by Liang. The distressed friends were so grateful for his life-saving grace that they were almost in tears. Liang said that there was no need to thank him. He only needed them to publicize the fact that he had abandoned his life of piracy and become a good citizen in their country to prove it. He also said that he would spend the rest of his life on this island.

The Commendable British Ship:

The British ship "La Qianpu Tai Nai" bravely ventured into the sea amidst the turbulent waves to rescue the crew of the Huayang ship. The British even broke the motorboat several tens of miles into the sea, but they continued to advance and finally rescued all one hundred and fourteen people onto the ship, providing them with Western food and letting them stay in the guest rooms, treating them with great care. The distressed friends were still unable to forget this even after arriving in Shanghai.

Friends' Travel Group Photo Exhibition 22

— Zhu Shouren

Photography is the most common art of modern times. Lovers of beauty regard it as an artistic tool. Those who delve into this art must first have a thorough understanding of its theory and technique, and then expand their innate aesthetic concepts through experience in order to express aesthetic feelings within the capabilities of photography. It cannot be achieved overnight, nor can it be faked. However, the application of photography is so wide that it is not as difficult as art photography to gain a glimpse of its secrets. In modern times, with the perfection of camera mechanics, those who know a little about it only need to open and close the lens to capture historical relics, scenic spots, buildings with historical value, and customs, human relationships, and social life with interest. The viewers are as if they are personally experiencing it. This is the special strength of photography and the goal of most photographers.

The Friends' Travel Group aims to use travel as a way to increase knowledge, and there are many members, including many skilled photographers. Every time they travel to a place, they obtain several fine photos, but they do not publicize them, limiting themselves to mutual appreciation among the members. Recently, in order to increase the interest in travel, they have collected about two hundred frames of films of famous scenic spots and historical sites taken by group members, and will hold the first Travel Photography Achievement Exhibition at the Guohuo Department Store (formerly the City Hall) on Nanjing Road from the 4th to the 6th of this month. The exhibition is planned by the group's staff members Yao Yuangan, Zheng Jiaguan, Shao Woyun, and Guo Xiqi. They also consulted with the Hu Boxiang and Boxian brothers, and I also participated in everything. Zhang Zhenhou and Zhang Zhongshan, giants of the Chinese community, and others have been specially invited to exhibit their works. In addition, Yu Pingke, Zhang Shaotang, Zhu Beigeng, and others have participated with excellent works (Juan Weng also has four recent works participating). Others, such as Lang Jingshan and Wang Dafo, have not had time to print their works due to the sudden rush of time and will wait for the second exhibition. Among the exhibits, the most numerous domestic scenes are from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, while there are also considerable works from Sichuan, Guangdong, Yan, and Lu provinces. Foreign scenes include India, Siam, Japan, and other places, all of which are souvenirs brought back by the group members' travels. Each frame is accompanied by an explanation. Reading the detailed illustrations is like wandering through the mountains and rivers. Those who do not have time to travel, why not take the time to visit, increase their knowledge, expand their horizons, and wash away the dust from their minds in the face of famous mountains and beautiful waters?

Hu Pu'an's Poet's Ambition 23

— Ma Xiexiong

Hu Yunyu, the Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, whose style name is Pu'an, is originally from Jing County, Anhui Province. Hu tilled the land himself from a young age, satisfied and without complaint. Later, because his hometown was plagued by bandits, he lived on the sea for many years. He did not want to live a city life. He was proficient in Chinese classics and served as a professor at various universities and in railway affairs. He never tired of serving the public and learning. Last spring, Ye Chucang, the Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, repeatedly invited him to take charge of the Jiangsu government. Hu repeatedly declined but was unsuccessful. After taking office, he maintained his integrity and self-discipline. This is where his reputation as "not loving money is the first achievement" came from. Hu is a passionate drinker and has always had a high tolerance for alcohol. Since he has been in charge of the Jiangsu government, his official duties have been laborious, and he has occasionally suffered from intestinal ailments, which have come and gone. Recently, he has abstained from alcohol for a long time. In the eastern corner of Hu's office, there are several thatched huts. He often rests there during his spare time, enjoying poetry and literature. Recently, he wrote four poems in the style of the Shanjian Xie Yao Gan and other rhymes, expressing his hatred for evil and his resentment towards the world. The poet's ambition is truly subtle and extraordinary, like a white crane soaring in the sky. The original poems are attached below and are divided into rhymes such as Yamen Zhai San Liang Jian, which are used in the Shanjian Xie Yao Gan and other rhymes.

[Poem 1]

Having three or two rooms in the Yamen, books accompany me and I am not stingy. It is always like this north and south of the Yangtze River, and I have traveled east and west for several times during the day.

It is pleasant to have flowers in the courtyard for my own enjoyment, and there are many difficulties in the four directions that are always related to me. Jin Jiao, Beigu, and San Shan are there, why use money to buy another mountain?

[Poem 2]

I am ashamed of not having the talent to manage the great help, and I am worried that I cannot descend. The rugged road turns into a winding path, and the sky is bleak with the shadows of wild geese.

I have already sighed that writing has misguided me into the world, and I have only burdened myself with wine to dispel my sorrow. The sound of beauty is cut off from a thousand miles away, and the spring waves are vast and green.

[Poem 3]

From afar, I pity my good homeland and nest, and the millet and millet are desolate on the path. Birds come to peck at the fruit in vain in search of food, and people have gone to plant melons and there are no gourds.

I am used to the house on the water, and my mother is busy divining. I also consider serving as an official only to be ridiculed. Last night, the spring breeze brought news, and the plum blossoms in the east garden are in bud.

[Poem 4]

Why abandon my talents to make a living and live up to the people of this place? I have fortunately entrusted myself to friends to comfort myself occasionally. I often compose poetry and find it difficult to remain silent, especially when I am sick and think of my hometown. I have other worries to entrust to my pillow.

I have tasted all the bitterness and hardship of the world, and I know that simple food is better than salt.

India Travelogue (42) 24

— Linghua

On the twenty-fifth, a Western woman took me by car to the Sarnath Mahayana Buddhist Assembly and Buddhist University. The Western woman is a Buddhist. Sarnath is where the Buddha first turned the wheel of Dharma and taught the five bhikkus. It is separated from Varanasi by a river. The river is named after a certain god's wife. From Benaras to Sarnath is about six English miles. The scenery outside the city along the way is quite scenic. Near Deer Garden, there are many mango trees forming forests. There are not many old houses, but the university has been built on a large scale. Currently, there are two monks and seven or eight disciples living here. There are no mountains, but it is a plain. In the past, it was called Deer Garden. Today, I still saw a deer nearby. Its horns did not take the usual shape, but rather formed a spiral, black in color. My visit to Deer Garden is different from my visit to Gaya. My trip to Gaya was specifically to visit the Buddha's relics, while my trip to Deer Garden was very hurried and I did not have time to examine it in detail. In short, when the Buddha first attained enlightenment, if he was speaking about the Avatamsaka Sutra, then Gaya was the place where he taught the Avatamsaka Sutra, while Deer Garden was the place where he taught the Small Vehicle scriptures, the Four Agamas. There is also a museum, which was established by the British to collect many broken pagodas and statues. Because I did not have time to examine the Buddha's relics in detail, I returned to Varanasi. The name of Varanasi is also detailed in the Lotus Sutra and other scriptures. I wrote a poem to commemorate it: "Before Deer Garden, I met a young deer, in the city of Varanasi, I visited a famous monk. All the tides return to the ocean, there will be an elephant king who should rise in response to the times."

On the twenty-sixth, I visited an Indian religious library. The religion has a Ramakrishna sect, which is a large sect in recent years. I first heard that a certain American woman was spreading its teachings. I also read the American woman's book and did not think it was unusual. When I read the biography written by the French Romain Rolland at the library, I realized that Krishna was a very unusual person. Romain Rolland is a famous world peace activist today. It can be said that Indian scholarship has the power to dominate the world. This sect was founded by his disciple Vivekananda. Vivekananda's statue is very majestic and sold everywhere. I have not yet studied its content. Recently, the statue makers have included him with Gandhi and Tagore as three heroes, but both teacher and disciple have died. In the evening, I walked along the Ganges under the moonlight. All my hospitality here is provided by Lawyer Mukherjee.

Rotary Club speech

The Turning Point in the Hawthorne Case (3) 25

— Cheng Xiaoqing

I had walked past more than a dozen storefronts on Qinghai Road when I suddenly seemed to hear faint footsteps following me from afar. At that time, I absolutely did not expect any danger or strange encounters. I was wearing a domestically produced spring tweed suit, and there was no large sum of money in my pockets. Moreover, I was carrying a black steel pistol in my pants pocket, so if any ignorant robbers had the nerve to try to touch me, they wouldn't necessarily get away with it. At this time, it was about half past eleven. Although Qinghai Road was quiet, Huanghe Road was still bustling with traffic. In fact, there was no reason to expect any accidents. While I was thinking quietly, I continued to walk slowly. The drowsiness in my mind had indeed lessened quite a bit, so I thought about having a cigarette. I took out a cigarette, paused slightly, struck a match, and started to smoke. However, the footsteps behind me seemed to quicken, getting closer and closer. Could I turn around and take a look? That was, of course, my prerogative, but at that awkward moment, such a turning movement would be seen as a sign of weakness and felt inappropriate. When my right hand threw the match's spent stub into the street, I took the opportunity to tilt my head and glance at the sidewalk behind me. What my optic nerve reported to my brain was a man of similar build to myself, wearing a suit, with a gray checkered spring jacket and chestnut-colored trousers underneath, and a dark brown bowler hat on his head. Both hands were tucked into the pockets of his jacket. This man seemed to be walking with his head down, and his steps were indeed very quick, only two or three steps away from me. This man's demeanor, except for his deliberately hurried pace which was somewhat suspicious, had nothing particularly out of the ordinary. I certainly shouldn't do anything rash, but amidst my perfect composure and ease, I couldn't help but be somewhat wary. While I wasn't afraid of robbers, I couldn't help but guard against detectives. As for adversaries in a relative position, in the past twenty years, I don't know how many extremely vicious and insidious criminals have fallen into our hands. It's not impossible that these people hold grudges and are secretly looking for opportunities to retaliate. Therefore, I deliberately slowed down my pace, preparing to let him pass first. My right hand involuntarily reached into my pants pocket.

Page 11

May 4th, 1931 (Third Page of Shen Bao) Monday (11th)

Education News

Sports

Jiangsu Province's 4th 26

Secondary School Joint Sports Meet, Day 3

Track and Field Events Conclude丨Twenty-Three New Records Created

Boys' Field Event Championship丨丨 Won by Jiangsu Provincial Su-zhong

Boys' Track Event Championship丨丨 Won by Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong

Girls' Track and Field Championship丨丨 Won by Jiangsu Provincial Yang-zhong Girls' School

Seven Team Sports Finals Today丨Closing Ceremony Held This Afternoon

Yesterday was the third day of the Jiangsu Province Secondary School's 4th Joint Sports Meet. The track and field events have concluded. The boys' schools Jiangsu Provincial Su-zhong won the field event championship, Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong won the track event championship, and the Jiangsu Provincial Yang-zhong Girls' School won the girls' track and field championship. A total of twenty-three new records were created for the conference track and field events. The results of the boys' and girls' A and B divisions were satisfactory and the crowds were very enthusiastic. The venue was orderly and well-managed. The finals of seven team sports for both boys and girls will be held today. We wonder which athlete will win the overall championship.

Let's See Who Gets the Championship

Boys' Group 27

Overall Championship

Field Event Championship Jiangsu Provincial Su-zhong has already won

Track Event Championship Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong has already won

Tennis Championship Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong or Jiangsu Provincial Tong-zhong

Basketball Championship Jiangsu Provincial Song-zhong or Jiangsu Provincial Shang-zhong

Volleyball Championship Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong or Jiangsu Provincial Shang-zhong

Soccer Championship Jiangsu Provincial Jing-zhong or Jiangsu Provincial Su-zhong

Women's Division 28

Overall Championship

Track and Field Championship: Won by Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou Girls' School

Tennis Championship: Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou Girls' School or Su Zhenhua

Basketball Championship: Jiangsu Provincial Suzhong or Songjiang Girls' School

Volleyball Championship: Xixi Jingzhi or Su Zhenhua

The Situation of Su Girls' School Defeating Shanghai Provincial

Su Girls' School defeated Shanghai Provincial 22-17

In the initial stages of the semifinal match between Su Girls' School and Shanghai Provincial, Su Girls' School was in a very disadvantageous position because their main players were also playing in the volleyball match at the same time. Su Girls' School suffered a major defeat in the first half, with a score of 5-11. Fortunately, reinforcements arrived, and Su Girls' School turned defeat into victory, tying the score at 17. Suzhong Girls' School Volleyball Team (Photo by Bao Mingshu)

The Process of Song Girls' School Defeating Jingzhi

Song Girls' School defeated Xixi Jingzhi 18-15. Songjiang Girls' School eliminated Wuxi Jingzhi with a score of 18-15. Referee Shao Ji. Song Girls' School's basketball skills were highly refined, their passing and coordination were excellent, and their defense and shooting were also well-executed. Although Xixi Jingzhi resisted with all their might, they were ultimately defeated. The halftime score was 11-3. In the second half, Song Girls' School used their reserve players, and the situation eased slightly. Finally, the main players were brought back, resulting in a final score of 18-15. Song Girls' School secured their spot in the finals and will face Su Girls' School this afternoon. Center Xu Jinzhu of Songzhong is capable of both offense and defense and is the most outstanding player on the entire court. The team has a well-rounded roster and will be a formidable opponent for Su Girls' School.

Women's Volleyball Semifinals

(1) Jingzhi defeated Su Girls' School

| 2-0 |

(2) Zhenhua defeated Jing Girls' School

| 2-1 |

Today's Finals: Jingzhi vs. Zhenhua

Su Girls' School suffers a crushing defeat against Jingzhi

Women's Volleyball: Jingzhi vs. Zhenhua Finals. Semifinal Results: (1) Jingzhi defeated Su Girls' School 2-0. Referee Huang Wenjian. (2) Zhenhua eliminated Jing Girls' School 2-1. Referee Xu Shaowu.

(1) Xixi Jingzhi defeated Su Girls' School 2-0. The match between Xixi Jingzhi and Su Girls' School was virtually a championship final. The two teams were the strongest in women's volleyball. Unfortunately, Su Girls' School was also competing in the women's basketball match at the same time, and their divided attention led to their defeat. It is a pity. However, Jingzhi's current skills are indeed better than Su Girls' School. They are reliable and have a well-organized team. Su Girls' School, on the other hand, still has uneven levels of skill. Center Zhang Yingfen is the most outstanding player on the first row, but there are occasional mistakes in the back row's support. The competition in the first game was fierce, with close scores. Su Girls' School even achieved a score of 15-14. However, consecutive errors led to Jingzhi's victory. In the second game, Su Girls' School still did not improve, and they suffered another defeat with a score of 21-7.

Zhenhua's skills are better than Jing Girls' School

Su Zhenhua defeated Jing Girls' School 2-1. Su Zhenhua Girls' School competed against Jing Girls' School in the volleyball semifinals at 4 PM. Jing Girls' School won. The result was 2-1, with scores of 11-21, 21-12, 21-12. Referee Xu Shaowu. Zhenhua secured their spot in the finals. Zhenhua's playing style seems more stable and their performance is excellent. Jing Girls' School made many mistakes, leading to their defeat.

Odds and Ends

Black Dust and White Powder Flying Everywhere

The wind was stronger in the afternoon and the weather was also hot. Dust was flying everywhere on the field. Spectators standing for a long time were either shouting that they couldn't open their eyes, or shouting that the dust was choking them, or shouting that their legs were sore. Especially for fashionable women, the red rouge and white powder that they put on before leaving home were exposed to the sun for a long time, plus a day of hot sweat, yellow oil, and a day of black dust in the strong wind. The misery was beyond description.

The Referee Only Asks About Today

After the results of the Men's Division B 200-meter final were announced, the height of the second-place winner, number 256, was measured. Because he was half an inch too tall, the referee reported that he was disqualified. He protested, "You didn't say I was too tall during yesterday's semifinal. Now you suddenly say I'm too tall. How could I have grown half an inch overnight?" The referee said, "I only ask about today."

Making the Defeated Feel Awkward

Director Hu is enthusiastic about sports. Despite his busy political affairs, he comes to the venue every day to watch the games. He sees the athletes and cheering squads, one group singing like orioles and swallows, and the other group roaring like the sea and mountains. Coincidentally, a reporter from this newspaper was nearby. Director Hu said to the reporter, "Cheering squads can only be used to cheer. Calling out cheers during athletic actions is acceptable. But calling out cheers after announcing the winners makes the defeated feel awkward. It is not the behavior of a virtuous person." These words are quite sufficient to advise those involved in sports.

Director Chen Hexi of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department and National Martial Arts Expert Sun Lutang (Photo by Bao Mingshu)

Spectators Crush the Barrier

Yesterday was Sunday, and there were probably 100,000 spectators in the entire venue. Although order was maintained by Boy Scouts and military police, the situation outside the venue was not as good. Many people were standing on the surrounding fences and orange crates. Even the reporter's seating area had people standing on the collapsing reed mat partitions and desks, making it difficult to prevent. Cigarette ashes and leftover food were scattered everywhere, creating a mess. The reporter could only endure and write quickly while hunched over his desk.

100-Meter Race with a Tin Can

Before the resting area for female athletes on the left corner of the podium, a tin can was placed on the field. At 1 PM, driven by the wind, it began its solitary 150-meter race. The sound of the can was sonorous, like a brass drum in the music, attracting the attention of the entire venue. Its speed was quite consistent. Although the time was not recorded when it reached the finish line, it was estimated to be around 3 minutes. The referee, because its speed was too slow, cancelled its qualification and expelled it from the venue.

200-Meter Race with a Military Cap

Fifteen minutes after the 100-meter race with the tin can, the 200-meter race with the military cap began. The starting point was also on the left corner of the podium. However, during the race with the military cap, there was a supervisor following behind to monitor the cap. The cap was round, and it rolled forward while racing, with a speed faster than the tin can. Its owner initially watched from behind. Seeing that it was going off course and running outside the area it should be running in, he went forward to try to correct it. However, the military cap was running enthusiastically and did not obey orders. Its owner then threatened it with a gun and knife. Only then did it become fearful and stop, allowing its fate to be decided.

News from the Shanghai Physical Education Instructors Association 33

The Shanghai Physical Education Instructors Association has held two preparatory meetings, and draft regulations have been prepared. The first general membership meeting is scheduled for 6:00 PM on May 5th (tomorrow) at the cafeteria of the YMCA on Sichuan Road.

Draft Regulations of the Association

(1) Name: The association is named the Shanghai Physical Education Instructors Association. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this association is to connect the physical education community in this city, research academics, enhance skills, jointly assist in the development of physical education in this city, and improve sportsmanship.

(3) Membership: Anyone meeting one of the following qualifications can become a member upon introduction by two or more members of the association and approval by the general meeting: (1) Basic Members: A. Current physical education instructors in secondary schools or above in this city. B. Current physical education administrative personnel in administrative agencies or public organizations in this city. (2) Supporting Members: A. Former physical education administrative personnel in administrative agencies or public organizations, or physical education instructors in secondary schools or above. B. Current sports journalists. (3) Honorary Members: A. Individuals enthusiastic about promoting physical education, invited to join by a resolution of the general meeting.

(4) Membership Fees: (1) Admission Fee: A one-time admission fee of ten yuan (as the association's fund) is required upon joining. (2) Annual Dues: Annual dues of six yuan (paid in full at once) are required each year.

(5) Officers: President, Vice President, Secretary, and Treasurer, one each. (6) Term of Office: The term of office for officers is one year, but re-elected officers may serve consecutive terms.

(7) Powers and Duties: 1. Powers and Duties of the President: (1) Overall management of association affairs and representation of the association in all external matters. (2) Appointment of directors of each group. (3) Convening of general meetings when necessary. 2. Powers and Duties of the Vice President: (1) Assisting the President in handling all association affairs. (2) Acting on behalf of the President when the President is unable to perform duties personally. 3. Powers and Duties of the Secretary: (1) Receiving and sending official documents and correspondence of the association. (2) Preserving official documents and important correspondence of the association. (3) Managing all books and records of the association. (4) Managing all reports of the association. (5) Presiding over all meeting records. 4. Powers and Duties of the Treasurer: (1) Managing the income and expenditures of the association. (2) Maintaining the books of the association. (3) Reporting the financial status of the association.

(8) Activities: The association is divided into (1) Research Group, (2) Editorial Group, (3) Sports Group, (4) Social Group. Each group has one director appointed by the President.

(9) Meetings: (1) The general meeting shall be held twice a year. (2) Regular meetings shall be held once a month. (3) Extraordinary general meetings may be convened by the President at the request of one-fourth of all members.

(10) Supplementary Provisions: Matters not covered in these regulations may be proposed by one-third of the members and amended by a resolution of the general meeting.

Minhang Central Primary School Sports Meet Report 34

Many Broke Previous Records

The Minhang Central Primary School in Shanghai County held its fourth annual sports meet on May 2nd. A total of 116 athletes participated. The results were quite impressive, especially in the field events, where many broke the previous county primary school sports records. For example, in the boys' A group, the high jump was 1.41 meters (previous county record: 1.31 meters), the shot put was 9.32 meters (previous county record: 7.89 meters); in the C group, the high jump was 1.24 meters (previous county record: 1.17 meters), the long jump was 4.34 meters (previous county record: 3.70 meters); in the D group, the high jump was 1.23 meters (previous county record: 1.11 meters), the long jump was 4.25 meters (previous county record: 3.90 meters); in the girls' B group, the long jump was 3.71 meters (previous county record: 2.85 meters). In the track events, Wu Yunzang of the girls' D group made the most significant improvement, with a time of 7 3/5 seconds in the 50-meter dash (previous county record: 8 1/5 seconds).
